<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">souderen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">souder</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">solidÅ</i>. The form <i><a href = vnd.unilang:solderen.html>solderen</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> originally Eastern Dutch and began to replace the form <i>souderen</i> starting in the late seventeenth century, which <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> apparently come to be regarded as substandard; this obsolete form existed until the early nineteenth century.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:solde.html>solde</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">solidus</i>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:sommige.html>sommige</a> (838)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">sommich</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">somich</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:som.html>som</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â</span><span class="mention-gloss">any, some</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">-ich</i>. The simplex <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:som.html>som</a></i> derives from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">sum</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â</span><span class="mention-gloss">any, some</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sumaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â</span><span class="mention-gloss">some</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> found also in other combinations such as <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:soms.html>soms</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">somtijds</i>.
</p><p>Related to English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">some</i>.
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">soprano</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span>literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â</span><span class="mention-gloss">high (voice)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***southside.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:southside.html>southside</a> (53204)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">south</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">side</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:southside.html>southside</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">southsides</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>The southern side of a building, street, area etc.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1999</b>,  Brendan <a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>O</a>'Carroll,  <cite>The <a href = vnd.unilang:mammy.html>Mammy</a></cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=VqU5HA3h3SICamp;lpg=PT15amp;dq=%22the%20northside%22amp;pg=PT15v=onepageamp;q=%22the%20northside%22amp;f=false">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">The retail section <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> two divisions <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:southside.html>southside</a></b> and the northside <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> with Grafton Street being the main shopping street of the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:southside.html>southside</a></b>, and <a href = vnd.unilang:henry.html>Henry</a> Street and Moore Street the flagships of the northside.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2012</b>,  Robert B. Stepto,  <cite>A Home Elsewhere: Reading African American Classics in the Age of Obama</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=KgZ0JBndgF0Camp;lpg=PA53amp;dq=%22southsides%22amp;pg=PA53v=onepageamp;q=%22southsides%22amp;f=false">[2]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">While certain <a href = vnd.unilang:details.html>details</a> indicate that this <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a black neighborhood up north in a Michigan city, quite possibly <a href = vnd.unilang:detroit.html>Detroit</a> as some have guessed, Morrison <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> deliberately not specific, allowing us to imagine that the "<a href = vnd.unilang:southside.html>Southside</a>" in her story could be any of a number of <b>southsides</b> created by the Negro migrations, including the <b>southsides</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> readers may have lived in.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2015</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:dale.html>Dale</a> A. Dye,  <cite>Run Between the Raindrops: Author's Preferred Edition</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=F7_YBQAAQBAJamp;lpg=PT98amp;dq=%22the%20southside%22amp;pg=PT98v=onepageamp;q=%22the%20southside%22amp;f=false">[3]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">What <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> apparently most galling to everyone not directly involved in the dirty fight on the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:southside.html>southside</a></b> of the Perfume River <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> that rattyass NVA flag still flying defiantly <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> the Citadel on the northside.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">spake</i>, an Ingvaeonic form of the more usual <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">speke</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*spÄka</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*spaikÇ­</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:spaan.html>spaan</a> (50681)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">spÃ¢en</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*spÄn</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*spÄnuz</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
